js-expandable clearfix js-listicle-body  css-listicle-body-2648116704"\n        ><div class="body-description" ><p>The chairman of the <a href="https://www.kait8.com/2020/10/06/craighead-co-republican-committee-leader-dies-covid-/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">Craighead County Republican Committee </a>in Arkansas has died from complications while fighting the coronavirus, reported KAIT8 News.</p><p>Steven Farmer\'s GOP committee hosted a social gathering with Sen. Tom Cotton (R-AR) and Rep. Louie Gohmert (R-TX), who just recovered from COVID-19, in mid-September. The Reagan Day event was photographed extensively, and it showed very few masks being worn and no social distancing.</p><p><br/></p>\n<div class="rm-shortcode" data-rm-shortcode-id="a613832fa9c0562afdbd9bd9fe26da59"><div class="fb-post" data-href="https://www.facebook.com/craigheadcorepublicans/posts/2639072309692892"></div></div>\n<p><br/></p>\n<div class="rm-shortcode" data-rm-shortcode-id="efeca602719b22f50b726eb41b821772"><div class="fb-post" data-href="https://www.facebook.com/craigheadcorepublicans/photos/a.2638774566389333/2638839296382860/?type=3"></div></div>\n<p>Farmer was admitted to the hospital on Sept. 18, just four days after the GOP event. He was put in the ICU and placed on a ventilator.</p><p>It is unclear when Farmer was first diagnosed with COVID-19, and whether he attended The Reagan Day gathering.</p><p>By Sept. 25, Farmer\'s doctor told the family that he was "very worried that dad was not going to make it through this," his daughter relayed.</p><p>Monday the doctors told her that her father had minimal brain activity and he died. He is survived by his wife, Judy Davis-Farmer, and their three daughters and several grandchildren.</p>\n<div class="rm-shortcode" data-rm-shortcode-id="dfe784a3b2ccb78140824b5a06f75d27"><div class="fb-post" data-href="https://www.facebook.com/audrey.haynie/posts/3799991073347905"></div></div>\n</div>\n        \n\n        \n\n\n\n    </div>\n\n\n\n<span class=""\n    data-elid="2648116704"\n    data-post-url="https://www.alternet.org/2020/10/arkansas-gop-county-chair-dies-from-covid-19-his-committee-hosted-a-mask-less-gathering-last-month/"\n    \n        data-authors="Sarah K. Burris, Raw Story"\n    \n    \n        data-headline="Arkansas GOP county chair died from COVID-19. His committee hosted a mask-less gathering last month"\n    >\n</span>\n<!-- ga_custom_dimensions: {u\'layoutId\': 11, u\'postDate\': 10, u\'postTags\': 9, u\'primaryTag\': 12, u\'authorName\': 7, u\'postID\': 13, u\'sections\': 8} -->\n    \n    \n    \n    \n    \n    \n    \n\n    \n \n    \n    \n    \n    \n    \n    \n    \n    \n    \n\n    \n    \n    \n    \n    \n\n<script type="application/json" id="post-context-2648116704">\n    {"customDimensions": {"8":"send","10":"10/06/2020","13":2648116704,"7":"Sarah K.
